provisions set forth in the Illinois plat act, 765 Illinois Compiled Statutes
205/1 et seq.
   (B)   All lot corners shall be monumented by survey monuments. Survey
monuments shall be a minimum of one-half inch (1/2") diameter iron pipe or
solid rod by thirty inches (30") in length with an identification cap affixed
to the top with the license number of the land surveyor setting the monument.
If disturbed or lost during construction of public improvements, such monuments
shall be replaced by, and at the expense of, the developer.
   (C)   All block corners, each end of all curves, points where curves change
radius, all angle points in a line, and two (2) opposite exterior corners of
the property platted shall be monumented with permanent monuments set in
concrete posts, the concrete having a minimum depth of thirty six inches (36")
and a minimum cross section of a five inch (5") diameter circle. Permanent
monuments shall have an identification cap affixed to the top with the license
number of the land surveyor setting the monument. If disturbed or lost during
construction of public improvements, such monuments shall be replaced by, and
at the expense of, the developer.
   (D)   All monuments shall be set such that they will not be moved by frost.
(2005 Code)
11-5-3: STREET IMPROVEMENTS:
   (A)   All streets and public ways shall be graded to their full width (as
specified in chapter 3 of this title) including side slopes, and to the
appropriate grade and shall be surfaced as provided in title 8, chapter 1 of
this code.
   (B)   Where storm sewers exist, concrete mountable V-type gutters with a
minimum width of twenty four inches (24") and a depth of six inches (6") shall
be installed. All improvements shall be constructed in conformance with the
requirements of title 7 of this code and shall be subject to inspection and
approval by the village engineer. (2005 Code)
11-5-4: WATER LINES:
   (A)   Where a subdivision is located within the village limits, each lot
therein shall be provided with a connection to the water utility system, said
water service to terminate not less than two feet (2') beyond the right of way
line. Fire hydrants shall also be installed in all subdivisions, within the
corporate limits, and the location of same shall be subject to review by the
village engineer and local fire department. The water supply system shall be
constructed to the standards and requirements, and be subject to the approval,
of the appropriate state and local authorities.
   (B)   In subdivisions outside the village limits, pending availability of a
public water supply, the subdivider shall demonstrate, through appropriate
tests, the likelihood of an adequate supply of potable water to every lot in
the subdivision at the time improvements are erected thereon. The installation
shall conform to standards and requirements and be subject to the approval of
the appropriate state and local authorities. (2005 Code)
11-5-5: SANITARY SEWERS:
   (A)   Where the subdivision is located within the village limits, each lot
therein shall be provided with a connection to a sanitary sewer, said sewer
connection to terminate not less than two feet (2') beyond the right of way
line. All connections to the village sewer system and the subdivision sewer
system shall comply with the provisions of title 7 of this code pertaining to
sewers and all construction of the system shall be subject to the standards and
requirements, and be subject to the approval, of the appropriate state and
local authorities.
   (B)   The village's engineers will perform:
      1.   Periodic observation of construction of sewer lines and manholes.
      2.   Observe the field measurement of installed sewer for grade and
alignment. Said field measurement shall be performed by the developer's
engineer. Developer's engineer shall notify the village's engineer of sanitary
sewer installation a minimum of twenty four (24) hours prior to the
installation of said sewer.
      3.   Observe sewer deflection and pressure tests. Developer's engineer
shall notify the village's engineer of sanitary sewer deflection and pressure
testing a minimum of twenty four (24) hours prior to said testing.
   (C)   In subdivisions beyond the village limits and within one hundred feet
(100') of the existing sanitary sewer lines, the subdivider may be required,
provided capacity exists, to install sewers in conformity with village
requirements. In such cases, until a connection can be made with the public
sewer system, the use of a primary sewage treatment plant will be permitted,
provided such disposal facilities are constructed in accordance with the
provisions of this code pertaining to sanitary sewage disposal and meet all
state requirements for sewage treatment and discharge. Otherwise, the
subdivider may install individual disposal devices for each lot at the time
improvements are erected thereon. All such individual sewage disposal systems
shall be constructed in accordance with regulations and requirements of the
appropriate department of health and under the direction and control of the
appropriate village and county authorities.
   (D)   All septic systems will be installed and maintained in accordance with
title 7 of this code and all applicable state and/or county requirements.
   (E)   Where sanitary sewers are required, the end of the sewer line shall be
installed to the appropriate boundary line as determined by the village
engineer, so as to allow for connection and extension by future adjoining
subdivisions. (2005 Code)
11-5-6: DRAINAGE:
The plat shall be laid out so as to provide proper drainage of the area being
subdivided in accordance with the provisions of title 7, chapters 3 and 4 of
this code. Preliminary plat approval shall be conditioned on subsequent
approval by the village engineer of all detailed engineering drawings, designs,
specifications, plans and calculations which shall be submitted to the village
by the developer prior to the start of work on improvements.
All detention ponds shall provide for emergency access approved by the board.
(2005 Code)
11-5-7: SIDEWALK IMPROVEMENTS:
Sidewalks shall be installed adjacent to all streets, and may be required along
other public ways, easements and common areas where significant pedestrian
traffic is anticipated or is to be encouraged. Sidewalks shall be graded and
surfaced as provided in title 8, chapter 1 of this code. (2005 Code)
